<div id="review_1546804828" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1546804828" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1546804828?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1546804828" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer987567059434994531">So, I took a little break from the Rock Chick series in order to let my Buddy Group catch up with me. Also, I needed a break from the alpha males in them. Most of you know me as an alpha female because I am, so sometimes it's hard for me to swallow all of the alpha male crap that other people find romantic. I don't find pushy, aggressive men attractive. I do, however, like men who are assertive, confident, and protective. It's a fine line and the Rock Chick guys cross over it a little too much f</span>
  <span id="freeText987567059434994531" style="display:none">So, I took a little break from the Rock Chick series in order to let my Buddy Group catch up with me. Also, I needed a break from the alpha males in them. Most of you know me as an alpha female because I am, so sometimes it's hard for me to swallow all of the alpha male crap that other people find romantic. I don't find pushy, aggressive men attractive. I do, however, like men who are assertive, confident, and protective. It's a fine line and the Rock Chick guys cross over it a little too much for my tastes. <br><br>All that said, I thought Hector was a much better hero than some of the past guys like Mace and Eddie. He was really careful with Sadie because she had been raped. BUT, once he got comfortable, he did piss me off when he told her that she couldn't dress how she wanted because she needed to cover herself up as his woman. And, later, after he gets in a bar fight with some guy who says something about Sadie, he blamed her way of dressing. But, the guy had known Sadie for a long time and had been having dirty thoughts about her for years. Does that mean that Sadie's outfit was to blame (she showed a little cleavage - gimme a break)? Hector used that guy's dickery to try and control Sadie. And, then he blamed her, which is shaming her. It's the oldest story in the world when women's clothing is an excuse for men's bad behavior. It's just wrong. So wrong...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455415774i/18099438._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> Yes!! You tell them, girlfriend!</i><br><br>Okay, and now let's talk about using rape as a plot device. Don't.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455415774i/18099439.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>There is way too much rape, threats of rape, almost rapes, and rapey talk in these books. Please stop!</i><br><br>And, finally, my last complaint: Sadie's use of the expression "Blooming Heck". First off, I don't think that's a thing.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455415774i/18099440._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've never heard an American use "blooming" as an adjective in general, but "blooming heck" makes it even worse. Stupider. More Stupid. Blooming Stupid. <br>And, she says it a lot. Like at least once a page. Just stop!<br><br>Okay, now the things I liked, cuz there were a few things.<br><br>First, I thought that Hector was actually pretty sweet and kind for the first half of the book. He didn't even try to kiss Sadie for a long time because he didn't want her to feel pushed and didn't want the rape PTSD to activate. He gave her time and space, and would ask her permission before he touched her. That gave him points (before he lost them on the telling her how to dress thing).<br><br>Second, we got some new characters in Ralphie and Buddy, Sadie's gay friends. They were more than awesome and super supportive of her. She felt like she had nobody who cared about her, but they did. She really just wouldn't allow anyone to get close. They swooped in after she was attacked and gave her what she needed to heal. They brought in a rape crisis counselor, but never pushed her. They allowed her to heal in her own time. They were amazing! I want to be their friend!<br><br>Finally, the whole Rock Chick world has developed and I love that we are seeing these relationships grow. There are lots of weddings and babies these days. I am just waiting for the next book to get Ally's story. Also, I wish there would have been a book that had Darius's story, but I think this series is done. That's a shame because he is definitely interesting.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="987567059434994531" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5084828872848466591"><b> 3.5-4 stars </b><br/><br/>Expectations. I normally don't go into books with them, but I had read that this book was very angsty and I was so excited to read it. Well...... it really wasn't all that angsty. Maybe the first 10% or so? After that not so much. And while I still enjoyed this book a lot, I was a bit let down because of the expectations I had going into this book. <br/><br/>This book is about Hector and Sadie.   <span id="freeText5084828872848466591" style="display:none"><b> 3.5-4 stars </b><br><br>Expectations. I normally don't go into books with them, but I had read that this book was very angsty and I was so excited to read it. Well...... it really wasn't all that angsty. Maybe the first 10% or so? After that not so much. And while I still enjoyed this book a lot, I was a bit let down because of the expectations I had going into this book. <br><br>This book is about Hector and Sadie. Sadie is the ice queen and daughter of a drug lord and Hector is the agent who brought her father down. Hector and Sadie were almost a thing, and then Hector made a mistake and expected Sadie to come back to him. Sadie finds herself in trouble and that's when Hector comes to the rescue.<br><br>This story has a very brutal beginning and while it was a lot, I loved that aspect of it. The rest of the book was sweet but a tad bit too long (as is per Kristen Ashley's style) which I normally don't mind, but in the 60-70% I found myself skimming. A very sweet ending that I think lots of readers will love. Actually I think readers will love the WHOLE book. My angst expectations held me back a bit to a like and not a love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1915491137" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17227497636850283028"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Love the males, dislike the females*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Re-read: 28.11.2017</u>
</b><br/>I don't know why I decided to re-read this one, but I guess I needed some KA alpha males. However, I still find the Rock Chicks so annoying and immature and I really dislike that in serious situations, things aren't serious enough. There's too much <i>joy</i> or <i>sassiness</i> to take it seriously, and those things really get on my nerves. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br/><b>What started out pretty great, got pretty boring at the end</b>... Really. It wa</span>
  <span id="freeText17227497636850283028" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Love the males, dislike the females*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 28.11.2017</u>
</b><br>I don't know why I decided to re-read this one, but I guess I needed some KA alpha males. However, I still find the Rock Chicks so annoying and immature and I really dislike that in serious situations, things aren't serious enough. There's too much <i>joy</i> or <i>sassiness</i> to take it seriously, and those things really get on my nerves. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br><b>What started out pretty great, got pretty boring at the end</b>... Really. It was awesome in the beginning. I loved <b>Sadie Marie Townsend</b> (29) attitude, her “<i>Ice Princess</i>”, and I loved her reaction to things. At least in the beginning. Eventually, as the story went, things got boring as Sadie <i>changed</i>, as in become more into herself, but as I dislike most of the <b>Rock Chicks</b> and Sadie become more like them, I lost interest. Though I adored <b>Lee Nightingale</b> with Sadie, and I wish we had gotten a stronger bond between them. Like a brother-sister bond. I love Lee, okay.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No really,” I whispered, letting the sweet, peaceful feeling steal over me. “It only matters if there’s someone to care if you don’t wake up. It’s okay if I don’t wake up because there’s no one to care.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Hector Chavez</b> (how old is he?) was hot, sexy, interesting and patient with Sadie. Which she both needed and didn't need. He gave her what she needed to <i>find</i> herself. Though Hector wasn't my favorite of the <b>Hot Bunch</b> in this series, I still liked him, but I didn't love him, just liked him a lot. Overall, the story was interesting enough, but <b>dragged out, and long</b>. On top of that it all, the story became all lovey-dovey and I'm not in for that. I like romance, but not too much of it. Final word is that the book was alright, but not my favorite.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life!' Vito exploded, making me jump. "Up and down, good and bad, birth and death, celebration and devastation. If you got any balls at all, you roll with the punches and get the fuck on with it, pardon my French.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487801604i/22052746.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series (Standalone), Book Seven<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Umm... Lee Nightingale?<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br><b>Rating</b> - 2.5/3 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

TIE FOR MY FAVORITE OF THE SERIES.</b> <br />Yep, I have 2 because I like them both in different ways. This is Favorite ½ lol. <br />I mean we get Hector “Oh my God” Chavez! This book made me cry and tear up multiple times and not just once but every time I re-read it. <br /><br />Sadie isn’t your average everyday girl, she grew up with a father who was head of crime and drugs. No real affection after the passing of her mother. She hasn’t had a real genuine friend all her life. So she protects herself with armor, whether that’s designer clothes or the facade of Sadie the Ice Princess. He is incredible, patient and finds Sadie utterly hilarious and I love that. <br />Hector is also Eddie’s brother so we see Blanca again yay I love when she showed up in Eddie and Jet’s book she was funny then and she is funny in this book as well. <br /><br /><i>“If he gets up before me, he tucks the covers around me so I won’t be cold.”</i> -Sadie<br /><br />Hector is just an all-around great character. <div id="review_1057747376" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1057747376" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1057747376?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1057747376" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5744257021677662168"><b>*** 3.75 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with my fellow KA addicts at BB&B</b><br/><br/>I am here to once again admit that I am a KA addict and I have no intention of going sober. Because her books are like junk food for the soul - you know that there is no nutritional value what soever, but you can't stop eating them no matter what.... <br/><br/>This book is all about recognizing who your friends are and being the best friend and person you could be. Sadie is known as the Ice Princess, the rich daddy's girl, who has it all and her ri</span>
  <span id="freeText5744257021677662168" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.75 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with my fellow KA addicts at BB&amp;B</b><br /><br />I am here to once again admit that I am a KA addict and I have no intention of going sober. Because her books are like junk food for the soul - you know that there is no nutritional value what soever, but you can't stop eating them no matter what.... <br /><br />This book is all about recognizing who your friends are and being the best friend and person you could be. Sadie is known as the Ice Princess, the rich daddy's girl, who has it all and her ride is payed for by her dad's dirty machinations in the criminal world. Hector was an undercover agent responsible for taking her dad down. One night during his undercover work the agent and the Princess had a moment of heat and neither of them can forget it. Months later he is working for Lee Nightingale Security and Sadie comes looking for protection from some really bad guys. Their paths cross again and they have to find a way to break the barriers between them in order to light the flames of something more than passion. Are they strong enough to deal with all their differences and would those around them let them be? Well that is why you have to read it, of course:-) <br /><br />I do have to warn potential readers that if you are sensitive to rape and violence, this might not be a read for you. This tale is brutal at times and I admit to crying in the beginning. However, KA surrounds us with old friends and hot, overprotective alpha males, puts the action in our favorite book/coffee Shop and all the love those characters exude towards us keeps us strong through the hardest experiences, including the usual kidnapping, fighting, and heavy fire shootouts. After all, it would not be a Rock Chicks book without them:-)<br /><br />I enjoyed this seventh installment in the series and am sad that we are getting to its conclusion with the next volume. So, let's hope we get to the finish line with a bang and be grateful for our little addiction support group in BB&amp;B!!?! Thanks to all my fellow buddy readers and see you next week:-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="5744257021677662168" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Nadia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25547640-nadia"><img alt="Nadia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587020307p2/25547640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/862399963?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nadia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nadia" href="/user/show/25547640-nadia">Nadia</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25547640-nadia?shelf=different-pov">different-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25547640-nadia?shelf=i-wanna-punch-the-hero-in-the-face">i-wanna-punch-the-hero-in-the-face</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25547640-nadia?shelf=bad-bad-book">bad-bad-book</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer862399963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9008129332038452699">This book didn't justify its high ratings, at least not to me. <br/>The beggining was heartbreaking and for me, the strongest part of the book. Afterwards, it went downhill. <br/><br/>Throughout the series we witness The Hot Bunch being very protective of their women, or women in general. So, there comes this girl, who everyone agrees looks like a fairy princess, and quite desperately asks for help and protection, for which she's denied for reasons, I honestly can't comprehend. What's even worse, they knew she</span>
  <span id="freeText9008129332038452699" style="display:none">This book didn't justify its high ratings, at least not to me. <br />The beggining was heartbreaking and for me, the strongest part of the book. Afterwards, it went downhill. <br /><br />Throughout the series we witness The Hot Bunch being very protective of their women, or women in general. So, there comes this girl, who everyone agrees looks like a fairy princess, and quite desperately asks for help and protection, for which she's denied for reasons, I honestly can't comprehend. What's even worse, they knew she was in danger and still didn't do anything. And then the girl everyone agrees looks like a fairy princess, got beaten up and raped. <br />Because of their behavior I lost my interest in this book, and well, in this series. I'm reading Ally's story half-heartedly. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[At least now I know Ally's sorry for how she behaved towards Sadie. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />You know, the sole reason I gave Rock Chick Renegade (book #4) a star more than I really wanted to, is how The Rock Chicks and The Hot Bunch worried about Jules after she got shot (otherwise I hated it and I hated the heroine). Every one of them was in the waiting room in the hospital, offering support, worrying about Jules, and she wasn't even that much part of the gang. And in this book, with how they acted towards Sadie in the beginning, they completely unmade every good opinion I had about them. <br />Of course, they tried to make it better later, but I just didn't feel the love. Not with The Rock Chicks, nor with Hector. <br /><br />I don't even want to start about Hector. Worst hero of the series, definitely.<br /><br />I loved Sadie's character a lot; how she could talk herself out of difficult situations or how she handled with everything happening to her. In my opinion, she should've stayed close to Ralphie and Buddy and send everyone else to hell.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9008129332038452699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9124913118096825191">Re-read: June 2019<br/><br/>First read April 23-25, 2012<br/><br/>One of my favorite parts of this book was the "Author's Note".<br/><br/>"And this, my loyal readers, is exactly what the entire series of 'Rock Chicks' is about, as Sadie learns in the story you are about to read.   <span id="freeText9124913118096825191" style="display:none">Re-read: June 2019<br /><br />First read April 23-25, 2012<br /><br />One of my favorite parts of this book was the "Author's Note".<br /><br />"And this, my loyal readers, is exactly what the entire series of 'Rock Chicks' is about, as Sadie learns in the story you are about to read. You are never alone, not when you have friends. <br />Learn from my stories and, through thick and thin, remember, if you have friends you are never alone".<br /><br />LOVED Hector Sadie together (amazing couple)!<br /><br />I loved how Sadie discovered she had friends (the Rock Chicks, the Hot Bunch, Tex and Duke), and that she had people she could count on who became her 'family'.<br />I liked reading Sadie's journey to find out 'who she really was' without having to wear all the different masks to protect her heart and her soul. <br />She truly did 'shine' when her true self came out.<br /><br />..and as always Kristen Ashley writes an 'amazing' Epilogue!!<br /><br />Really enjoyed this read, can't wait to read Ally's story!<br /><br /><br /><br />Second read December 2014<br /><br />Really enjoyed this re-read, and Rock Chick Regret is still one of my favorites.<br /><br /><br />￼</span>

<div id="review_1181373307" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1181373307" />
    <a title="Sharon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39569169-sharon"><img alt="Sharon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1422218548p2/39569169.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1181373307?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon" href="/user/show/39569169-sharon">Sharon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1181373307" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1448375770396608203">This one really bugged me because of the shoddy treatment of rape & rape survivors & also because of issues with the story Here's why:<br/><br/>1. Sadie gets raped, there is no explanation of what happened. Rape is very painful & traumatic & I feel that since KA chose to use her rape as part of the story then she should have at least shown what she went through. This would get the reader emotionally invested in a "I feel your pain/ struggle" kind of way. <br/><br/>2. Sadie asked Lee for help while Hector was in the</span>
  <span id="freeText1448375770396608203" style="display:none">This one really bugged me because of the shoddy treatment of rape &amp; rape survivors &amp; also because of issues with the story Here's why:<br /><br />1. Sadie gets raped, there is no explanation of what happened. Rape is very painful &amp; traumatic &amp; I feel that since KA chose to use her rape as part of the story then she should have at least shown what she went through. This would get the reader emotionally invested in a "I feel your pain/ struggle" kind of way. <br /><br />2. Sadie asked Lee for help while Hector was in the room before her rape ordeal. They say NO &amp; treat her horribly. the Rock chicks also treat Sadie coldly &amp; ignore her. She gets raped &amp; suddenly they are all BFFs, life is fun &amp; all is forgiven! I expected MORE GROVELLING! After all the shit they put her through I wanted them to EARN their way back into her life. Sorry but NO. <br /><br />3.The Rock chicks, the hot bunch &amp; Hector all spread far &amp; wide to anyone who is willing to listen to them that Sadie has been raped. This by FAR was what left a bad taste in my mouth. Many rape survivors have a hard time verbalising what happened to them &amp; many feel like talking about what happened is akin to going through a SECOND RAPE. Her so called friends spreading this story to everyone barely a MONTH after the incident strikes me as cold, mean, callous &amp; just plain shitty behavior. It's not their story to tell, it's not their trauma to tell! With "friends" like this who needs enemies?<br /><br />4. Sadie &amp; Hector start dating and a sexual relationship between these two starts a MONTH after she has gone through a brutal rape. She still has her cast on for gods sakes!! WHO DOES THAT? granted, rape survivors all heal at varying levels but already, taking into account that the man she's supposed to be having sex with let her walk out of the door unaided to her rape..strikes me as unbelievable! What compounds this for me is Hector never apologises for his prior treatment of her. it's as if it never happened!<br /><br />5. Hector treated Sadie horribly before the rape &amp; we never see them talk about this. It hurt her very much but they never resolve this issue. It seems like they just ignore it. The mistreatment at the hand of the rock chicks is similarly not dealt with. In fact, there's a scene where Sadie is at the gallery, the girls come over to see her &amp; she ignores them. In the book, she is made to feel GUILTY for brushing them off! I think this could have been better handled. KA could have taken this dynamic, the tension between the characters &amp; turned it into literary gold! I would have loved to see Sadie angry, how she deals with her rape, her mistrust of the rock chicks &amp; hot bunch &amp; how they manage to get her to trust them, Hector showing himself as worthy of her...all of this instead of jumping right to the sex &amp; skipping over all the necessary healing. I give 2 stars because I really enjoyed reading the interraction between Sadie &amp; her gay pals.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1448375770396608203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_312057479" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/312057479" />
    <a title="SoBeA" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2125909-sobea"><img alt="SoBeA" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1238854199p2/2125909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/312057479?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SoBeA" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SoBeA" href="/user/show/2125909-sobea">SoBeA</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer312057479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2780474015987701986">Okay, so this is one of those books I don't quite know how to rate...Though I'm pretty sure I've got an overall dissenting opinion of it.....<br/><br/>On the one hand it's a typical enjoyable KA title,( at least the last half, )<br/>On the other, there are two reasons I can't say that I honestly liked this. So ok.<br/><br/>One. <br/>blooming Heck. I know it's stupid, and I know there are people who don't like to curse....and I've no problem with them. But blooming heck? Seriously? <i> blooming</i> heck? And it's used through the wh</span>
  <span id="freeText2780474015987701986" style="display:none">Okay, so this is one of those books I don't quite know how to rate...Though I'm pretty sure I've got an overall dissenting opinion of it.....<br /><br />On the one hand it's a typical enjoyable KA title,( at least the last half, )<br />On the other, there are two reasons I can't say that I honestly liked this. So ok.<br /><br />One. <br />blooming Heck. I know it's stupid, and I know there are people who don't like to curse....and I've no problem with them. But blooming heck? Seriously? <i> blooming</i> heck? And it's used through the whole damn book? Who takes a heroine seriously when she keeps saying blooming heck? Whats next, sprouting poop.? Jeez.<br /><br />Two.<br />Okay this point is more serious. The rape. It's treated like a plot device rather then the serious issue it is....and it laughs in the face of everything we're taught about rape and rape victims. <br />The scene itself is never described...I can understand that, I'm sure writing it, would be beyond difficult, just like reading it would be. However, the absolute lack of any details whatsoever, make it feels like it's glossed over, Like we don't get the full emotional impact we should...in Ava's book, even though she isn't fully raped ( meaning no penetration), she's violated, and we get the scene...which helps us connect with the story and with her. But, in Regret, since we don't get the scene, we never really connect with Sadie, at least I didn't... It felt like she hardly reacted at all..yes there were a few scenes showing her issues, but they're few and far between and she gets over them somewhat quickly. <br /><br />Then there's the fact that with the exception at the begining of the book, and the times she yells about it, she doesn't come off as a rape victim. She could have easily been the victim of some other crime. a mugging, a beating, etc<br /><br />Oh and my biggest issue....I know rape victims are all different and react in various way..but 30 days? Most victims can take years to recuperate and 30 mother fucking days after her attack, she's out partying? Getting set up on dates? Seriously? Being forced into situations /relationahips ( because apparently being raped didn't take enough of her choices away, her new gay bestie ( who's stereotypical gayness, irritated me beyond all blooming heck) , decided to make all her decisions for her) again and again. Having the fact that she's been raped announced to all and fucking sundry, and her not having an issue with it? None of that seems synonymous with what we learn about rape victims. So yeah, they're all different, but I cant help but feel, like the issue doesn't get the due diligence that it rightly deserves...<br /><br />And the fact that it's the rock chicks themselves that go about making sure everyone in their social circle knows she was raped...well it makes me think a whole lot less of them...it's a little too naively callous, not to mention flat out insensitive. <br /><br />Oh and the hot bunch? They're supposed to be all about women in trouble and they turn her over to someone else...And to some small, tiny degree, I even get why...but really, if lee's the big badass, who takes care of women, why wouldn't he have called this associate he sends Sadie( the h) to just to give him a heads up? I would have loved me to be in lees head when they found out about the rape...even after the fact. ..there's a bit where he feels bad, but then he gets over it pretty dammed quickly...<br /><br /><br />The whole thing leaves me with a bad taste. Thinking it over, I'd say <s> 2 stars</s> 1 star. I tried giving it 2, as I like KA, but I think I'm a little too offended to give it anything other then a one. <br /><br />Side note: The first review I wrote for RC Regret, was a hell of a lot worse, chock full of anger and curse words, and full on non stop ranting and soap boxing so I think I've toned it down to a somewhat coherent review, but I may still come back and try and clean this up... but at the mo' I think I'm taking a break from KA...At least til I can forge how angry this book made me.<br /><br /><br />ETA: it's even worse now, because I'm reading another <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13491780-winter-of-the-wolf" rel="nofollow noopener"> book </a>with has a rape victim in it, but is treating he whole topic better than KA did.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2780474015987701986" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_341918480" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/341918480" />
    <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward"><img alt="Kellie Maddox-Ward" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366371073p2/7309666.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/341918480?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kellie Maddox-Ward" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward">Kellie Maddox-Ward</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward?shelf=hot-hot-alpha-s">hot-hot-alpha-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward?shelf=queen-ka">queen-ka</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer341918480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer753028762718433854"><i>
  <b>“I call them as I see ‘em. He’s Hispanic…” Ralphie lifted one hand and then continued, “And he’s hot.” He lifted his other hand and then shoved them together like he was squeezing an accordion. “Hence, Hispanic Hottie.” </b>
</i><br/><br/><b>= = > I may swear and have small spoilers! .Don’t say you weren’t warned < = =</b> <br/><br/>This is how Ralphie see’s the rest of the Hot Bunch. <br/><br/>Hawaiian Hottie <br/>Hispanic Hottie<br/>Just Plain Old Hot Hottie<br/>Alaskan Hottie <br/>Surfer Dude Hottie <br/>African American Hottie <br/>Native American Hottie <br/>(Not in</span>
  <span id="freeText753028762718433854" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“I call them as I see ‘em. He’s Hispanic…” Ralphie lifted one hand and then continued, “And he’s hot.” He lifted his other hand and then shoved them together like he was squeezing an accordion. “Hence, Hispanic Hottie.” </b>
</i><br /><br /><b>= = &gt; I may swear and have small spoilers! .Don’t say you weren’t warned &lt; = =</b> <br /><br />This is how Ralphie see’s the rest of the Hot Bunch. <br /><br />Hawaiian Hottie <br />Hispanic Hottie<br />Just Plain Old Hot Hottie<br />Alaskan Hottie <br />Surfer Dude Hottie <br />African American Hottie <br />Native American Hottie <br />(Not including Lee, Hank, Eddie, Jack) <br /><br />I’ve said it before but I will say it again. KA is a G-E-N-I-U-S! <br /><br />This book was fantastically written! It takes you into very dark issues, Rape, abduction, drug lords etc. The way it is written you have information to form your own idea without it being spelled out for you. It is dark enough to get the VERY Serious issues across but enough humour to know that you are reading a KA book. <br /><br />Things I loved about this book - - <br /><br /><b>Hector </b> -- **Sigh** He is literally a knight in shining armour. We not only find out the reason he left the DEA and joined Lee’s team, we fall in love with him for it. The way he takes care of Sadie is just beautiful. He is def a wildcard that I wasn’t expecting to love but I sure as hell do now! He’s an alpha like the rest of them down to the core, but he is also incredibly sweet and gentle as well. <br />I loved that he knew what he wanted and was a bit of a rebel. Fighting to stay in the hospital room, that it took all the boys to hold him back when Sadie went off at him and ran to her house. I just love him! <br />We all know that Eddie used the term <i>“Mamita”</i> with Jet but my heart absolutely melted when he not only used <i>“Mamita”</i> but also <i> Mi Cielo</i> <i>mi Corazon</i> and I got all happy and fuzzy when he finally said <i>Y tea mo tambien, mi cielo.</i> (I love you too my sky) The guy is just AMAZING! <br /><br /><b>Sadie </b> - Will of Fucking Steel alright! My heart broke for her after she went through. That she had no family. No friends. She was the most vulnerable of all the rock chicks, BUT she was also the strongest in my eyes! She took what came at her. Let it affect her for a few minutes; and then BANG she bounced back. I loved that she was naive and just clueless sometimes. I loved that she loved Veronica Mars and after seeing Lottie she wanted to be a stripper. I loved that she wanted to be a rock star like Stella. That she wanted to sand Hector’s floor. That when she was kidnapped she was thinking about what colour to paint Hector’s room! In the end I just loved her. She really did make me smile and I was so happy that she now officially a rock chick! And her wedding/Christmas presents made me smile and laugh. Oh and also the way she stood up to Blanca and helped Jet out. <br /><br /><b>Daisy </b> She really stepped up to the plate in this one. I have always loved her. And I REALLY want to know in details the story of her and Marcus (who I also love!) but when she beat the shit out of Harvey I was in Hysterics! You little fire cracker you! Even though they weren’t friends, that she was there for Sadie as soon as Marcus told her what happened! <br /><br /><b>The Rock Chicks </b> - Hands down best bunch of chicks ever! I want to be them! <br /><br /><b>The Hot Bunch </b> ***HUGE MO’FO SIGH** Aren’t they just the SHIT?! The way they looked after each one of the girls and also Sadie was just .. *sigh* I don’t just mean by protecting but making her one of them, the hugs, temple kisses etc. <br /><br /><b>Ralphie and Buddy </b> The best! LOVE THEM! <br /><br /><b> Just everything! </b><br /><br />I can’t wait to read about Ally and Ren! Especially after the end of the book where they get in an argument. What’s that all about?! Oh now to play the waiting game! <br /><br /><br />Some of my Fav parts were: (Sorry Highlighted a bit in this one! LOL)<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Then before I could stop it, to my horror, I started crying.<br />Really! Where was my Ice Princess? Why did she come along when she wasn’t wanted and disappeared when I needed her? She was beginning to really annoy me.<br />When the Ice Princess didn’t show, with no other choice so he wouldn’t see me cry, I shoved my face in his neck.<br />He dropped to the side on his back taking me with him. He rolled us and then we were lying on the couch, me snug between the heat of him and the soft back of the couch.<br />One of his arms held me close at the waist; the other hand cupped the back of my head and held my face to his throat.<br />“Let me take care of you,” he whispered through my sobs.<br />“Okay,” I whispered through my sobs too, too tired to fight it anymore<br />…………………………………<br />Take hold of life and live it beautiful...<br /><br />…………………………….<br />"And this, my loyal readers, is exactly what the entire series of 'Rock Chicks' is about, as Sadie learns in the story you are about to read. You are never alone, not when you have friends. <br />Learn from my stories and, through thick and thin, remember, if you have friends you are never alone". –Kristen Ashley (Authors Note)<br />……………………………..<br />"Sadie?"<br />"What?"<br />"You with me?"<br />I blinked in confusion and said, "Yes." And I was, wasn't I? I was standing in his arms for goodness sake.<br />"This is Sadie?" Hector went on.<br />I blinked again. "Yes."<br />"My Sadie?" he kept at it.<br />This time I blinked for a different reason.<br />His Sadie? Was there a Hector's Sadie? Was I Hector's Sadie? Did Hector think I was his Sadie?<br />Oh…my…God.<br />Before I could process what he said or get close to processing what that meant, I watched him smile, then he bent his head and kissed my lips.<br />"Yeah," he said, his face an inch away. "It's my Sadie."<br /><br />………………………………..<br />“Well Buddy’s in the kitchen grating cheese like a grating fool. We’ve decided to do nacho’s. Ralphie’s gaze moved to Hector and he informed him, “It’s the food of your people.” <br />………………………………..<br />“Okay kids,” Ralphie said, trailing me. “Don’t be too late. Don’t do any drugs, drive smart and even if all the other kids are doing, think twice. If you’re going to be over your curfew then make sure you call your’s Daddies or we’ll get worried.” <br />……………………………….<br />“Mamita, only you can find your way. I just wanna be along for the ride.” <br />………………………………<br />“Hector? You call him Hector?” <br />“Well, I can hardly call out ‘Agent Chavez, oo Agent Chavez,’ when he makes me climax now can I?” <br />………………………………<br />“Life!” Vita exploded, making me jump. “Up and down, good and bad, birth and death, celebration and devastation. If you got any balls at all, you roll with the punches and get the fuck on with it. Pardon my French.”<br />…………………………….<br />“This is a Rock Chick Powow. The rules of a Rock Chiclk Powwow are, you gotta be a girl, a gay, Duke or Tex. No one else allowed.” <br />“Why are Duke and Tex allowed?”<br />“Who knows? Who cares? It just happened, It was organic. But now its Rock Chick Law.” <br />……………………………..<br />You been through what you been through and you’re still standin’. Lotsa women wouldn’t only bend, they’d break but you didn’t do either and you’re still standin’. You were my daughter, I’d be so fuckin’ proud, I’d shout it from the rooftops. I figure, so would your Ma. And you can take that to the fuckin’ bank!” - - - - God I love TEX! Lol <br />…………………………….<br />“Maybe I should go put on my ragged white dress and stone necklace and you can put on your leopard skin tunic and we can pedal in our stone car to the roadhouse before you go bowling with Barney and I go shopping with Betty, Fred.” </b>
</i><br /></span>

As much as Luke/Ava's makes me laugh, this one has me in tears from beginning to end!<br/><br/>Re-Read January 2016 <br/><br/>SO much of this book annoys me. The annoying, and unnecessary "Natalie" scene. The way everyone treats Sadie at the beginning, and the way everyone spreads what happened to her around. Yet there is something that gets me every time, and I end up loving this thing despite all the above! *lol* </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=stalker">stalker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=latino-hero">latino-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=private-investigator-hero">private-investigator-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280350816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6362181096442738650">So, Hector Hispanic Hottie Chavez meet Sadie Townsend – daughter of an incarcerated druglord and total Ice Queen<br/><br/>We first met Hector back in Rock Chick Renegade when he was working deep undercover as a DEA agent to bring down a druglord – namely Sadie’s father. His mission was successful and he quit shortly after and become one of the Nightingale Hot Bunch. Whilst undercover he met Sadie and realised the Ice Queen façade was a strong defence against a loveless world.<br/><br/>Sadie’s story is tragic – her </span>
  <span id="freeText6362181096442738650" style="display:none">So, Hector Hispanic Hottie Chavez meet Sadie Townsend – daughter of an incarcerated druglord and total Ice Queen<br /><br />We first met Hector back in Rock Chick Renegade when he was working deep undercover as a DEA agent to bring down a druglord – namely Sadie’s father. His mission was successful and he quit shortly after and become one of the Nightingale Hot Bunch. Whilst undercover he met Sadie and realised the Ice Queen façade was a strong defence against a loveless world.<br /><br />Sadie’s story is tragic – her mother disappeared when she was 11. She was left with her father who made her rich in material goods but poor in emotional security. She’s taught herself to put on her ‘Ice Princess’ as protection against getting hurt. Once, just once, when a little bit inebriated, she let this persona slip and shared a passionate moment with Hector whilst he was still undercover. This was enough to let Hector see the real Sadie, his Sadie, and decide she was going to be his woman but he waited. Waited for her to come to him. Big mistake.<br /><br />When she does eventually come, it’s to Nightingale Investigations to ask for protection against the Balducci Brothers who are keen to take over her now incarcerated father’s position and see her as the ultimate prize. Inexplicably, Lee turns her away and something very, very bad happens to Sadie that evening.<br /><br />At this point, Sadie doesn’t care if she lives or dies; she just wants the pain to end. During her recovery, she finds that she actually does have people that care about her and, after giving her a month to recuperate; Hector begins to pursue Sadie in earnest. Just like his brother Eddie, the way he whispers endearments to her in Spanish is sizzling hot – really made me sigh lustfully. His care and patience with Sadie is so touching – she’s been badly hurt, is emotionally brittle and he knows he needs to take things slowly and his patience and care with her is so very beautiful to read.<br /><br /><i>Then before I could stop it, to my horror, I started crying.<br />Really! Where was my Ice Princess? Why did she come along when she wasn’t wanted and disappeared when I needed her? She was beginning to really annoy me.<br />When the Ice Princess didn’t show, with no other choice so he wouldn’t see me cry, I shoved my face in his neck.<br />He dropped to the side on his back taking me with him. He rolled us and then we were lying on the couch, me snug between the heat of him and the soft back of the couch.<br />One of his arms held me close at the waist; the other hand cupped the back of my head and held my face to his throat.<br />“Let me take care of you,” he whispered through my sobs.<br />“Okay,” I whispered through my sobs too, too tired to fight it anymore. </i><br /><br />Le sigh!!<br /><br />Most of the story revolves around an emotional journey for Sadie from a seemingly unloved and battered Ice Queen with Hector helping her along the way with care, tenderness and almost infinite patience. I fell a lot in love with Hector during this one.<br /><br />Of course, the danger is still there for her and we have the usual multiple kidnappings and gunbattles before Sadie is safe and she and Hector get their HEA.<br /><br />A heartfelt 5 stars romantic suspense for the beautiful romance.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6362181096442738650" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3733940-gretchen-about-that-story?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3733940-gretchen-about-that-story?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3733940-gretchen-about-that-story?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100046743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1259626554788061025"><b>This was just THE BEST! I absolutely loved Hector and Sadie's story. </b>So much depth and emotion, I couldn’t get enough. <br/><br/>Hector and Sadie were such strong characters. Hector was so wonderful, sweet, sexy, caring, and so very understanding but also very alpha male but in a quieter way. I absolutely adored Sadie. She had such a tough exterior, and I loved every little step she took as she opened up. Sadie was a truly strong woman and I loved watching her break down and being built back up. I love th</span>
  <span id="freeText1259626554788061025" style="display:none"><b>This was just THE BEST! I absolutely loved Hector and Sadie's story. </b>So much depth and emotion, I couldn’t get enough. <br /><br />Hector and Sadie were such strong characters. Hector was so wonderful, sweet, sexy, caring, and so very understanding but also very alpha male but in a quieter way. I absolutely adored Sadie. She had such a tough exterior, and I loved every little step she took as she opened up. Sadie was a truly strong woman and I loved watching her break down and being built back up. I love them together. Things definitely got emotional between the two but they could also be super sweet, playful, and way sexy. I thought there was a great balance with everything.<br /><br />There was a lot of drama happening, lots of layers, and a ton of characters at play. I love the intricacies of it all. <b>I thought the pace was excellent, wonderful build, and really great writing.</b> Kristen Ashley is an amazing story teller.<br /><br />I just have to say, I love how the Rock Chicks were represented in this book. Sadie's story is different than any other and I loved that all the women where there for her but giving her space. Really reading what she needed and not going full on Rock Chick until she was ready. I love when things click for Sadie and she really lets her hair down and you can see those Rock Chick friendships in full effect. The Hot Bunch are awesome as always but I loved seeing their sweeter tender sides when dealing with Sadie. I loved the new characters that were introduced as well, Ralphie and Buddy were a great addition.<br /><br />This was just an excellent, excellent read. <b>I was so wrapped up in it all, hanging on every word, it was hard to out down.</b> Great drama and turmoil, lots of tension but so full of love and heart. Loved the end with the recaps of who is doing what, everything made me so happy and I cannot wait for Aly and Ren’s story next. <br /><br />Another must read story in the Rock Chick series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1259626554788061025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3466949078" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Elle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/88949895-elle"><img alt="Elle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591041608p2/88949895.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3466949078?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle" href="/user/show/88949895-elle">Elle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88949895-elle?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88949895-elle?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3466949078" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer126293022151655633">In the words of Michael Scott: OMG OKAY ITS HAPPENING EVERYBODY STAY CALM STAY FUCKING CALM EVERYBODY CALM DOWN<br/><br/>We finally got this masterpiece, it only took 6 books. <br/>Okay where do I even start?<br/><br/><br/>The main character of this book is Sadie Townsend and she is the daughter of a drug lord. Her mother left her life by disappearing when Sadie was 11 years old. During the years growing up, Sadie built a reputation as the The Ice Princess. She was known for being cold and not letting anyone in and she is de</span>
  <span id="freeText126293022151655633" style="display:none">In the words of Michael Scott: OMG OKAY ITS HAPPENING EVERYBODY STAY CALM STAY FUCKING CALM EVERYBODY CALM DOWN<br /><br />We finally got this masterpiece, it only took 6 books. <br />Okay where do I even start?<br /><br /><br />The main character of this book is Sadie Townsend and she is the daughter of a drug lord. Her mother left her life by disappearing when Sadie was 11 years old. During the years growing up, Sadie built a reputation as the The Ice Princess. She was known for being cold and not letting anyone in and she is determined to keep it that way.<br /> <br />Fast forward and she is now 29 years old, her father is in prison leaving no one to take over his business. This leaves Sadie with a target on her back. One night she is drugged, beaten up and raped and ends up in the arms of Hector Chavez. A handsome mexican man working for Nightingale Investigations. He is able to get to the real Sadie that is hiding behind The Ice Princess and he is determined to keep her safe. <br /><br />Okay so I loved this. I really liked Sadie, she wasn’t annoying like all the other rock chicks and she understood that people tried to keep her safe, which the other girls didn’t understand. <br /><br />Then we have Hector. Where do I even begin? He is this badass guy that in reality is a huge marshmallow. A cinnamon roll. A fluffy cloud. He is so precious I want to hug him. The romance was perfect, it wasn’t forced like the other books, this felt normal and good. <br /><br />This is the reason I kept reading this series. I knew the books had the potential to be this good and now I finally got the book I wanted. </span>
  <a data-text-id="126293022151655633" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+t5tx7cmn5I8KoFEXXn77gRs44S5Ye+8vsl+xsCj1Lr/rqrwrvqoWwGEYLiDJx/4PhsgSxGwaWwLIELF1VSIgQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley">About Kristen Ashley</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4169620901644227452">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText4169620901644227452" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
